***willa.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:willa.html>willa</a> (25509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wiljô</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">willio</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">willo</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">willo</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wille.html>Wille</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">vili</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">vilja</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:willa.html>willa</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang">willan</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>desire, inclination, will
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latinx mention e-example" lang="ang">wilġesīþ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">willing companion</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latinx mention e-example" lang="ang">willwyrdan</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be complaisant</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>wish, desire
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latinx mention e-example" lang="ang">wilcuma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">desired guest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>pleasure, delight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latinx mention e-example" lang="ang">wilboda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">angel, messenger of joy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>will, intent</li></ol>
</body>

***willen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a> (166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wiljaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*welh₁-</i>. The variant spelling <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wouden.html>wouden</a></i> goes back to early <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wolde</i><i>(n)</i>, following the standard <i>ol</i> gt; <i>ou</i> transformation in Middle Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to want, to desire</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the past tense</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wou.html>wou</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>wish</b> I could (do) that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wou.html>Wou</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wouden.html>wouden</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often used in the past tense, depending on the region, but mostly in informal language. In formal language, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilden.html>wilden</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> preferred by many, although <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wou.html>wou</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wouden.html>wouden</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> recognized as correct standard Dutch.
</p>

***willkommen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>willkommen</a> (85978)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">willekomen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">willechomen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wiljakumô</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welkom.html>welkom</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">welcome</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">velkommen</i>, and other Germanic forms. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bienvenu</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">benvenuto</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">bienvenido</i>, possibly Germanic calques.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>willkommen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>welcome <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">received with gladness</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Du <a href = vnd.unilang:bist.html>bist</a> mir <a href = vnd.unilang:immer.html>immer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>willkommen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You’re always <b>welcome</b> to my house.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>Das</a> ist eine <b>willkommene</b> Gelegenheit.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>welcome</b> opportunity.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The German word <i>gern</i> can translate English welcome in some constructions.  This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not used with a following infinitive; to say “You are welcome to use my car", use a sentence such as <i>Du kannst gern <a href = vnd.unilang:mein.html>mein</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>Auto</a> nehmen.</i></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>willkommen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>welcome
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>Willkommen</a></b> in Deutschland!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Welcome</b> to Germany!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>Willkommen</a></b> am Bodensee!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Welcome</b> to Lake <a href = vnd.unilang:constance.html>Constance</a>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>Willkommen</a></b> auf Helgoland!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Welcome</b> to Heligoland!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>Willkommen</a></b> auf meiner Webseite!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Welcome</b> to my website!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>Willkommen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bei.html>bei</a> meinen Eltern!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Welcome</b> to my parents’ house!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>As can be seen from the examples above, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>willkommen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> construed with prepositions of position (not movement) corresponding to the object. Thus, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">in</i> with countries and cities, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">an</i> with <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a> of water, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:bei.html>bei</a></i> with people, etc., as they are generally used to indicate position.</li>
<li>The preposition <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> may be used with events and activities: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>Willkommen</a> zur Weinprobe!</i> (“Welcome to the winetasting!”) However, one may also follow the general rule and use <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:bei.html>bei</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">auf</i>, or whatever preposition of position <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> appropriate.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>willkommen</a></strong> (<i>class 4 strong</i>, <i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">willkommt</b>, <i>past tense</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">willkam</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>willkommen</a></strong></b>, <i>past subjunctive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">willkäme</b>, <i>auxiliary</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:haben.html>haben</a></b>)</li>
<li><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>willkommen</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">willkommt</b>, <i>past tense</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">willkommte</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">willkommt/gewillkommt</b>, <i>auxiliary</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:haben.html>haben</a></b>)</li></ul>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to welcome</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:willkommen.html>Willkommen</a></span></li></ul>
</body> 
***willow.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:willow.html>willow</a> (7756)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wilwe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">welew</i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wilghe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">weliġ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wiligaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wylch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilg.html>wilg</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wel-ik-</i> (compare (Arcadian) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἑλίκη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">helíkē</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hittite_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hittite language">Hittite</a></span> <i class="Xsux mention" lang="hit">𒌑𒂖𒆪</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hit-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">welku</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twist, turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:willow.html>willow</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">willows</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various deciduous trees or shrubs in the genus <i>Salix</i>, in the <a href = vnd.unilang:willow.html>willow</a> family Salicaceae, found primarily on moist soils in cooler <a href = vnd.unilang:zones.html>zones</a> in the northern hemisphere.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1912</b> January,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zane_Grey" class="extiw" title="w:Zane Grey"><a href = vnd.unilang:zane.html>Zane</a> Grey</a>,  chapter 8, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Riders_of_the_Purple_Sage" class="extiw" title="w:Riders of the Purple Sage"><a href = vnd.unilang:riders.html>Riders</a> of the Purple Sage: A Novel</a></cite>, New York, N.Y.; London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harper_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Harper (publisher)">Harper amp; Brothers Publishers</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/6868219">6868219</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Instead there were the white of aspens, streaks of branch and slender trunk glistening from the green of leaves, and the darker green of oaks,">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> and through the middle of this forest, from wall to wall, <a href = vnd.unilang:ran.html>ran</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:winding.html>winding</a> line of brilliant green which marked the course of cottonwoods and <b>willows</b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>The wood of these trees.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cricket<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cricket bat.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">baseball<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> 1800s</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The baseball bat.</li>
<li>A rotating spiked drum used to open and clean cotton heads.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">withy</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:willow.html>willow</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">willows</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">willowing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">willowed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To open and cleanse (cotton, flax, wool, etc.) by means of a <a href = vnd.unilang:willow.html>willow</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To form a shape or move in a way similar to the long, slender <a href = vnd.unilang:branches.html>branches</a> of a <a href = vnd.unilang:willow.html>willow</a>.
<ul><li><b>1928</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Byron" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robert Byron">Robert Byron</a>, <i>The Station: Travels to the Holy Mountain of Greece</i>, Chapter 12,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.net.au/ebooks14/1403311h.html">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd><b>Willowing</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the rough cobbles of the little <a href = vnd.unilang:pier.html>pier</a> stepped a thin, <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> figure, adorned with a silver nannygoat’s beard and bobbling <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> interrupted by the rim of a pair of pince-nez.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1930</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Talbot_Mundy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Talbot Mundy"><a href = vnd.unilang:talbot.html>Talbot</a> Mundy</a>, <i>Black Light</i>, Chapter 7,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://gutenberg.net.au/ebooks06/0609211h.html">[2]</a></sup>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:joe.html>Joe</a>’s impulse <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> to sketch her, with her shadow <b>willowing</b> beyond her on the mouse-gray paving-stone; but his left fist, obeying <a href = vnd.unilang:instinct.html>instinct</a>, remained clenched behind his back <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1985</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Martin_Booth" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Martin Booth">Martin Booth</a>, <i>Hiroshima <a href = vnd.unilang:joe.html>Joe</a></i>, New York: Picador, p. 394,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=lYXWAAAAQBAJamp;printsec=frontcoverv=onepageamp;qamp;f=false">[3]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> floating a foot under the surface. The <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:holes.html>holes</a>. The mouth <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a slit cavern of darkness. The hair <b>willowed</b> around the scalp.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2013</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dean_Koontz" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Dean Koontz"><a href = vnd.unilang:dean.html>Dean</a> Koontz</a>, <i>Wilderness</i>, Bantam Books,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=sVE0AQAAQBAJamp;printsec=frontcoverv=onepageamp;qamp;f=false">[4]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>The draft-drawn smoke <b>willowed</b> down through the hole and across my face, but I didn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> worry about coughing or sneezing.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li>Originally northern British usage, from the 1960s. Probably the simple use of a proper name as a pet name; compare <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>dick</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:fanny.html>fanny</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>peter</a></i>. Unlikely to be a contraction of <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i>membrum virile</i>, male member (that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, the <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a>), a Latin term used in English in the nineteenth century.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">hypocoristic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> childish</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> childish</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Term of abuse.</span></li></ol>

***wimper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wimper.html>wimper</a> (52683)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wimbrauw</i>, contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wintbrauwe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wintbrāwa</i>. The first element <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unknown but presumed to be related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἴονθος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">íonthos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; the second element <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brēwō</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wenkbrauw.html>wenkbrauw</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eyebrow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wimper.html>wimper</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> native in some Dutch dialects; its adoption into the standard language (19th c.) probably under influence of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wimper.html>Wimper</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wimper.html>wimper</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wimpers.html>wimpers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wimper.html>wimpertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>eyelash</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wimper.html>wimper</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:anatomie.html>anatomie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:haartje.html>haartje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:langs.html>langs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rand.html>rand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ooglid.html>ooglid</a></li></ol>

***winden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:winden.html>winden</a> (7379)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:winden.html>winden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*windan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*windaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winden.html>winden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to wind (turn coils of something around)</li></ol>

***windscherm.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:windscherm.html>windscherm</a> (58526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wind</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scherm.html>scherm</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">screen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense “windscreen of an aircraft” derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">windscreen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:windscherm.html>windscherm</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:windschermen.html>windschermen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:windscherm.html>windschermpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A windbreak <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">screen to protect against the wind</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The windscreen of an aircraft.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">regenscherm</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:winger.html>winger</a> (58525)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wing</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:winger.html>winger</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">wingers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One of the casks stowed in the wings of a vessel's hold, being <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> than such as are stowed more amidships.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> hauled out a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:winger.html>winger</a></b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:grog.html>grog</a>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An offensive player who plays on either side of the center.
<dl><dd><i>The center passed to the left <b><a href = vnd.unilang:winger.html>winger</a></b>, who shot and scored.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> October 1,  Alistair Magowan,  “Man Utd 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 0 Norwich”, in  <cite>BBC Sport</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/eng_prem/15045317.stm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"The pattern of the game could have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> different if Anthony Pilkington <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> one of two chances either side of United's opener.<br />But the Norwich <b><a href = vnd.unilang:winger.html>winger</a></b> shot wide when clean through and saw another effort hit the post on 75 minutes.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***winkel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a> (1100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">corner</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*winkilaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weng-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend, bow, arch, curve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>Winkel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wincel</i>. The meaning "shop" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived from the meaning "corner in which merchandise <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> stalled".
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkels.html>winkels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkeltje.html>winkeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>shop (an establishment that sells goods to the public).
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boetiek.html>boetiek</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:handel.html>handel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> corner, as in <a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaak</a></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a></strong>
</p>

***winkelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:winkelen.html>winkelen</a> (3498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkelen.html>winkelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to shop, to go shopping (typically for luxury goods, not for groceries: compare <a href = vnd.unilang:boodschappen.html>boodschappen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***winkelhaak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaak</a> (78007)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">winkelhake</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">try square, carpenter's square</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haak.html>haak</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Serurista_ortilo.jpg/250px-Serurista_ortilo.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Serurista_ortilo.jpg/375px-Serurista_ortilo.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Serurista_ortilo.jpg/500px-Serurista_ortilo.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1840" data-file-height="840" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>Winkelhaak</a></i><br />Try square</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg/250px-Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="300" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg/375px-Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg/500px-Winkelhaak_in_textiel.jpg 2x" data-file-width="901" data-file-height="1081" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaak</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:textiel.html>textiel</a></i><br />Winkel-hawk in textile</div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winkelhaak.html>winkelhaakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>try square; or, generally, any <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of square used by masons and <a href = vnd.unilang:carpenters.html>carpenters</a> to measure right angles, such as a steel square or a carpenter's square</li>
<li>a rectangular tear or cut in a piece of clothing or other fabric, in the form of a try square.</li></ol>

***winnen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:winnen.html>winnen</a> (686)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:winnen.html>winnen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">winnan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*winnaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wenh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to strive, desire, wish, love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winnen.html>winnen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive or intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to win, to triumph, to be victorious (in)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to acquire</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to extract, to refine, to harvest (from base materials such as ore or crops)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***wiskunde.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiskunde.html>wiskunde</a> (4232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier Modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wisconst</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">art of what <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> known</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wis.html>wis</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-kunde</i>. Purism introduced by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simon_Stevin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Simon Stevin"><a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> Stevin</a> in the 16th century to replace the Dutch word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mathematica.html>mathematica</a></i> which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a borrowing from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:mathematica.html>mathematica</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiskunde.html>wiskunde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>mathematics</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">-kunde</span></li></ul>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:wetenschap.html>wetenschap</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:formele.html>formele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:studie.html>studie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:patronen.html>patronen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:structuren.html>structuren</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiskundig.html>wiskundig</a> (21739)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiskunde.html>wiskunde</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiskundig.html>wiskundig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiskundig.html>wiskundiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">wiskundigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mathematical
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fysische.html>fysische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:chemie.html>chemie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tracht.html>tracht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:chemische.html>chemische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verschijnselen.html>verschijnselen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wiskundige.html>wiskundige</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:modellen.html>modellen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verklaren.html>verklaren</a>.</i>  |  Physical chemistry attempts to explain chemical phenomena by means of mathematical <a href = vnd.unilang:models.html>models</a>.</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wisselen.html>wisselen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wissalon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wihslōną</i>. ***wit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a> (1863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwittaz</i>. The geminate <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unexpected as the usual <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwītaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱweytos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shine; bright</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The geminate <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes explained as being the result of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kluge%27s_law" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kluge | s law">Kluge's law</a>, thus from a Pre-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kweyd-nos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:witter.html>witter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">witst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>white
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wand.html>wand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The (inner) wall <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>white</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly Surinam</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> having a white skin colour, light-skinned <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">see usage note</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Surinam</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> having a relatively light skin colour</li>
<li>legal</li>
<li>pure, untainted</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clear-lighted, not dark at all
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewenst.html>gewenste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verscheen.html>verscheen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klaar.html>klaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The long-wished-for day appeared, very clear and <b>white</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Recently, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> come to be used in continental Dutch by some (associated with social justice movements) to refer to a specific skin colour, i.e. to light-skinned people of apparent mostly European descent. Traditionally, the adjective <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> used there for this purpose, and this usage <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> by far the most widespread in the Netherlands and Belgium.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">wijting</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:witten.html>witten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>witje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> white <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">color</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>Wit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleuren.html>kleuren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ineens.html>ineens</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">White <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> all colors at once.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>short for <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doelwit.html>doelwit</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">goal, target, the white in a <a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>bullseye</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Myn <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:adam.html>Adam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> zyn <a href = vnd.unilang:afkomst.html>afkomst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bederven.html>bederven</a>. (in <a href = vnd.unilang:lucifer.html>Lucifer</a>, by Vondel)</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My <b>goal</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to corrupt <a href = vnd.unilang:adam.html>Adam</a> and his origin.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-, second- and third-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:witten.html>witten</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:witten.html>witten</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*witją</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knowledge, reason</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyd-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">see, know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wis.html>wis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knowledge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Witz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:witten.html>witten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>witje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ability to think and reason</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> knowledge</li></ol>

***withers.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:withers.html>withers</a> (66523)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From dialectal English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wither</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">against</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <i>wither-</i>)  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-s</i>; see <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">with</i>. So-named because it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the part of the horse that pushes <i>against</i> a load. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Widerrist</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:withers.html>withers</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">wider</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">against</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:rist.html>Rist</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wrist</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:withers.html>withers</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>normally plural</i>, <i>singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en">wither</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The part of the back of a four-legged animal that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> between the shoulder <a href = vnd.unilang:blades.html>blades</a>; in many species the highest point of the body and the standard place to measure the animal's height. <span class="defdate">[from 1580]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>Even</a> in the plural, this noun refers to one object. The synonymous singular, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wither</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> less common.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:withers.html>withers</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Third-person singular simple present indicative form of <span class="mention" lang="en">wither</span></span></li></ol>
</body>
